nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtyaVdhaMaṅg
naraṃ caiva narottamamVdhaMaṅg
devīṃ sarasvatīṃ caivaVdhaMaṅg
tato jayam udīrayetVdhaMaṅg
dvaipāyanauṣṭhapuṭaniḥsṛtam aprameyaṃVdhaMaṅg
puṇyaṃ pavitram atha pāpaharaṃ śubhaṃ caVdhaMaṅg
yo bhārataṃ samadhigacchati vācyamānaṃVdhaMaṅg
kiṃ tasya puṣkarajalair abhiṣecanenaVdhaMaṅg
namo vyāsāya guraveVdhaMaṅgalt
sarvajñāya maharṣayeVdhaMaṅgalt
pārāśaryāya śāntāyaVdhaMaṅgalt
namo nārāyaṇāya teVdhaMaṅgalt
kṛtābhiṣekaṃ tanayamVdha
rājñaḥ pārīkṣitasya haVdha
draṣṭum abhyāyayuḥ prītyāVdha
śaunakādyā maharṣayaḥVdha
tān āgatān sa rājarṣiḥVdha
pādyārghyādibhir arcitānVdha
sukhopaviṣṭān viśrāntānVdha
tatkathābhiḥ kṛtāhlādaḥVdha
praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥVdha
śatānīko 'tha papracchaVdha
nārāyaṇakathāṃ parāmVdha
yam āśritya jagannāthamVdha
mama pūrvapitāmahāḥVdha
vipakṣāpahṛtaṃ rājyamVdha
avāpuḥ puruṣottamāḥVdha
mama yena pitāmahaḥVdha
parīkṣit prāṇasaṃyogaṃVdha
devadevena lambhitaḥVdha
tasya devasya māhātmyaṃVdha
śrutaṃ subahuśo mayāVdha
kaḥ stotum īśas tam ajaṃVdha
yasyaitat sacarācaramVdha
brahmāṇḍam udare śayamVdha
rudraḥ krodhodbhavo yasyaVdha
prasādāc ca pitāmahaḥVdha
tasya devasya kaḥ śaktaḥVdha
pravaktuṃ vā vibhūtayaḥVdha
so 'ham icchāmi devasyaVdha
tasya sarvātmanaḥ prabhoḥVdha
śrotum ārādhanaṃ yenaVdha
nistareyaṃ bhavārṇavamVdha
kenopāyena mantrair vāVdha
rahasyaiḥ paricaryayāVdha
dānair vratopavāsair vāVdha
japyair homair athāpi vāVdha
ārādhitaḥ samastānāṃVdha
kleśānāṃ hānido hariḥVdha
śakyaḥ samārādhayituṃVdha
tan naḥ śaṃsata sattamāḥVdha
vidyānām api sā vidyāVdha
śrutānām api tac chrutamVdha
rahasyānāṃ rahasyaṃ tadVdha
yena viṣṇuḥ prasīdatiVdha
mantrāṇāṃ paramo mantroVdha
vratānāṃ tan mahāvratamVdha
upoṣitaṃ hi tac chreṣṭhaṃVdha
yena tuṣyati keśavaḥVdha
sā jihvā yā hariṃ stautiVdha
tac cittaṃ yat tadarpaṇamVdha
tāv eva kevalau ślāghyauVdha
yau tatpūjākarau karauVdha
sujanma deham atyantaṃVdha
tad evāśeṣajanmasuVdha
yad eva pulakodbhāsiVdha
viṣṇor nāmābhikīrtanātVdha
sā hānis tan mahac chidraṃVdha
sā cāndhajaḍamūkatāVdha
yan muhūrtaṃ kṣaṇaṃ vāpiVdha
vāsudevo na cintyateVdha
nūnaṃ tat kaṇṭhaśālūkamVdha
athavā pratijihvikāVdha
rogo vānyo na sā jihvāVdha
yā na vakti harer guṇānVdha
santy anekā bilās tadvacVdha
śrotram apy alpamedhasāmVdha
dattvāvadhānaṃ yac chabdeVdha
vinaiva harisaṃstutimVdha
puruṣāṇāṃ viceṣṭitamVdha
janmany aviphalā saikāVdha
yā govindāśrayā kriyāVdha
apāram abhidhāvatāmVdha
ekaḥ kṛṣṇanamaskāroVdha
muktitīrasya deśikaḥVdha
sarvaratnamayo meruḥVdha
sarvāścaryamayaṃ nabhaḥVdha
sarvatīrthamayī gaṅgāVdha
sarvadevamayo hariḥVdha
evam ādiguṇo bhogaḥVdha
śruto me bahuśo siddhaiḥVdha
gīyamānas tathāparaiḥVdha
so 'ham icchāmi taṃ devaṃVdha
nārāyaṇam aśeṣasyaVdha
jagato hṛdy avasthitamVdha
ārādhayitum īśānamVdha
anantam amitaujasamVdha
śaṃkaraṃ jagataḥ prāṇaṃVdha
tan mamādya muniśreṣṭhāḥVdha
prasādayitum icchataḥVdha
prasādaṃ kartum arhataVdha
tasyaitad vacanaṃ śrutvāVdha
bhaktim udvahato hareḥVdha
paritoṣaṃ paraṃ jagmurVdha
munayaḥ sarva eva teVdha
sarve ca te muniśreṣṭhāVdha
bhṛguśreṣṭhaṃ ca śaunakamVdha
yathārthaṃ bhagavaṃs tasmaiVdha
kathyatām ity acodayanVdha
sarvajñānanidhiḥ sphītasVdha
tvam atra bhṛgunandanaVdha
tamodīpas tapodhanaVdha
evam ukto munivaraiḥVdha
prītyā tasya ca bhūpateḥVdha
bhaktyā ca devadevasyaVdha
śithilaṃ bhagavān athaVdha
pratyuvāca mahābhāgaḥVdha
śaunakas taṃ mahīpatimVdha
yat pṛcchasi mahīpālaVdha
kṛṣṇasyārādhanaṃ pratiVdha
tad ihaikamanāḥ śṛṇuVdha
anādimat paraṃ brahmaVdha
vyāpi yat sarvabhūteṣuVdha
sthitaṃ sadasataḥ paramVdha
pradhānapuṃsor ajayorVdha
yataḥ kṣobhaḥ pravartateVdha
nityayor vyāpinoś caivaVdha
jagadādau mahātmanoḥVdha
tatkṣobhakatvād brahmāṇḍaVdha
sṛṣṭihetur nirañjanaḥVdha
ahetur api sarvātmanaḥVdha
jāyate parameśvaraḥVdha
pradhānapuruṣatvaṃ caVdha
samupaiti tataś caivaVdha
brahmatvaṃ chandataḥ prabhuḥVdha
tataḥ sthitau pālayitāVdha
viṣṇutvaṃ jagataḥ kṣayeVdha
rudratvaṃ ca jagannāthaḥVdha
svecchayā kurute 'vyayaḥVdha
tad ekam akṣaraṃ dhāmaVdha
paraṃ sadasator mahatVdha
praṇipatya paraṃ padamVdha
pravakṣyāmi yathā pūrvaṃVdha
matpitrā kathitaṃ mamaVdha
tasyāpi kila tatpitrāVdha
tasmai cāha kilośanāḥVdha
tenāpi bhṛgum ārādhyaVdha
prāptam ārādhanaṃ hareḥVdha
sakāśād brahmaṇaḥ prāptaṃVdha
bhṛguṇāpi mahātmanāVdha
marīcimiśraiś ca purāVdha
param etan maharṣibhiḥVdha
prāptaṃ sakāśād devasyaVdha
brahmaṇo vyaktajanmanaḥVdha
yogaṃ brahmā paraṃ prāhaVdha
maharṣīṇāṃ yadā prabhuḥVdha
tadā jagatpatir brahmāVdha
praṇipatya maharṣibhiḥVdha
sarvaiḥ kilokto bhagavānVdha
ātmayoniḥ prajāhitamVdha
yo yogo bhavatā proktoVdha
prāptuṃ śakyaḥ sa tv anekaiḥVdha
janmabhir jagataḥ pateVdha
viṣayā durjayā nṝṇāmVdha
indriyākarṣaṇāḥ prabhoVdha
vṛttayaś cetasaś cāpiVdha
capalā cātidurdharāḥVdha
rāgādayaḥ kathaṃ jetuṃVdha
śakyā varṣaśatair apiVdha
na yogayogyaṃ hi manoVdha
bhavaty ebhir anirjitaiḥVdha
alpāyuṣaś ca puruṣāVdha
brahman kṛtayuge 'py amīVdha
tretāyāṃ dvāpare caivaVdha
kimu prāpte kalau yugeVdha
bhagavaṃs tvam upāyajñaḥVdha
prasanno vaktum arhasiVdha
anāyāsena yenemamVdha
uttarema bhavārṇavamVdha
duḥkhāmbumagnāḥ puruṣāḥVdha
prāpya brahma mahāplavamVdha
uttareyur bhavāmbhodhiṃVdha
tathā tvam anucintayaVdha
evam uktas tadā brahmāVdha
kriyāyogaṃ mahātmanāmVdha
teṣām ṛṣīṇām ācaṣṭaVdha
narāṇāṃ hitakāmyayāVdha
ārādhayata viśveśamVdha
nārāyaṇam atandritāḥVdha
tam ajaṃ jagataḥ patimVdha
śuśrūṣābhir aharniśamVdha
vratopavāsair vividhairVdha
brāhmaṇānāṃ ca tarpaṇaiḥVdha
tais taiś cābhimataiḥ kāmairVdha
ye ca cetasi tuṣṭidāḥVdha
ārādhayata keśavamVdha
tanniṣṭhās tadgatadhiyasVdha
tatkarmāṇas tadāśrayāḥVdha
taddṛṣṭayas tanmanasaḥVdha
sarvasmin sa iti sthitaḥVdha
samastāny atha karmāṇiVdha
tatra sarvātmanātmaniVdha
saṃnyasyadhvaṃ sa vaḥ kartāVdha
etat tad akṣaraṃ brahmaVdha
pradhānapuruṣāv ubhauVdha
yato yasmin yathā cobhauVdha
sarvavyāpiny avasthitauVdha
paraḥ parāṇāṃ paramaḥVdha
sa ekaḥ puruṣottamaḥVdha
yasyābhinnam idaṃ sarvamVdha
yac ceṅgaṃ yac ca neṅgatiVdha
tam ārādhya jagannāthaṃVdha
mokṣakāraṇam avyaktamVdha
acintyam aparigrahamVdha
kriyāyogena mucyateVdha
iti te brahmaṇaḥ śrutvāVdha
rahasyam ṛṣisattamāḥVdha
narāṇām upakārāyaVdha
yogaśāstrāṇi cakrireVdha
muktikāryāṇy anekaśaḥVdha
ārādhyate jagannāthoVdha
paramātmā hṛṣīkeśaḥVdha
sarveśaḥ sarvabhāvanaḥVdha
tāni te nṛpaśārdūlaVdha
sarvapāpaharāṇy ahamVdha
vakṣyāmi śrūyatām anyadVdha
rahasyam idam uttamamVdha
uttāram icchatāṃ tasmādVdha
bhṛśaṃ yan nāntarair apiVdha
viṣṇupotaṃ vinā nānyatVdha
kiṃcid asti parāyaṇamVdha
uttiṣṭhaṃś cintaya hariṃVdha
vrajaṃś cintaya keśavamVdha
bhuñjaṃś cintaya govindamVdha
svapaṃś cintaya mādhavamVdha
evam ekāgracittas tvaṃVdha
saṃśrito madhusūdanamVdha
saṃsārāmbhas tariṣyasiVdha
anantam īḍyaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇaṃVdha
jagadvidhātāram ajaṃ janitryamVdha
samāśritā ye harim īśitāraṃVdha
teṣāṃ bhavo nāsti hi muktibhājāmVdha
śrūyatāṃ kuruśārdūlaVdha
saṃvādo 'yam anuttamaḥVdha
ambarīṣasya rājarṣeḥVdha
saha devena cakriṇāVdha
ambarīṣo mahīpālaḥVdha
pālayann eva medinīmVdha
udvigna eva dvandvāntamVdha
abhīpsuḥ puruṣarṣabhaḥVdha
devadevāt sa govindādVdha
abhīpsur dvandvasaṃkṣayamVdha
tapas tepe nirāhāroVdha
gṛṇan brahma sanātanamVdha
tasya kālena mahatāVdha
bhaktim udvahataḥ parāmVdha
tutoṣa bhagavān viṣṇuḥVdha
sarvalokapatiḥ prabhuḥVdha
sa rūpam aindram āsthāyaVdha
tam uvāca mahīpatimVdha
vāraṇendragatis tadāVdha
rājarṣe vada yat kāryaṃVdha
tava cetasy avasthitamVdha
varado 'ham anuprāptoVdha
varaṃ varaya suvrataVdha
evam uktas tato rājāVdha
vilokya ca puraṃdaraṃVdha
pratyuvācārghyam udyamyaVdha
svāgataṃ te 'stv iti prabhoVdha
nāham ārādhayāmi tvāṃVdha
tava baddho 'yam añjaliḥVdha
varārthināṃ tvaṃ varadaḥVdha
prayacchābhimatān varānVdha
varārthāya tvayānyaiś caVdha
kriyate nṛpate tapaḥVdha
sa kim arthaṃ tvam asmattoVdha
na gṛhṇāsy abhivāṃchitamVdha
na varārtham ayaṃ yatnasVdha
tvatto devapate mamaVdha
viṣṇor ārādhanārthāyaVdha
viddhi māṃ tvaṃ kṛtodyamamVdha
ahaṃ hi sarvadevānāṃVdha
trailokyasya tatheśvaraḥVdha
pālayanti mamaivājñāmVdha
ādityādyāḥ sadā surāḥVdha
ādityā vasavo rudrāVdha
nāsatyau marutāṃ gaṇāḥVdha
prajānāṃ patayaḥ sādhyāVdha
viśvedevā maharṣayaḥVdha
kurvanty ete mamaivājñāṃVdha
matto hi ko 'nyo varadaḥVdha
pratigṛhṇīṣva vāñchitamVdha
tvam indraḥ satyam evaitadVdha
devas tribhuvaneśvaraḥVdha
tvayāpi prāptam aiśvaryaṃVdha
yatas taṃ toṣayāmy ahamVdha
trailokyaṃ tava deveśaVdha
vaśe yasya mahātmanaḥVdha
saptodare śayā lokāsVdha
tam īśaṃ toṣayāmy ahamVdha
yasya tvam amaraiḥ sarvaiḥVdha
samavetāḥ sureśvaraVdha
dehaprāpto 'ntarastho vaiVdha
taṃ namāmi janārdanamVdha
nimeṣo brahmaṇo rātrirVdha
unmeṣo yasya vāsaraḥVdha
tam īḍyam īśam ajaraṃVdha
praṇato 'smi janārdanamVdha
yo hartā jagato devaḥVdha
kartā pālāyitā ca yaḥVdha
trayasyāsya ca yo yonisVdha
taṃ viṣṇuṃ toṣayāmy ahamVdha
hiraṇyakaśipuḥ pūrvaṃVdha
hiraṇyākṣaś ca te ripuḥVdha
tavānukampayā yenaVdha
hatau daityau nato 'smi tamVdha
balināpahṛtaṃ śakraVdha
dattaṃ yena purā tavaVdha
trailokyarājyaṃ taṃ baddhvāVdha
taṃ namāmi janārdanamVdha
prasīda śakra gaccha tvamVdha
aham apy atra saṃsthitaḥVdha
tapas tapsye jagannāthaṃVdha
draṣṭuṃ nārāyaṇaṃ harimVdha
evam uktas tatas tenaVdha
śakrarūpī janārdanaḥVdha
punar apy āha taṃ kopātVdha
pārthivaṃ tapasi sthitamVdha
yadi madvacanād adyaVdha
na bhavāṃs tyakṣyate tapaḥVdha
vajraṃ te prahariṣyāmiVdha
budhyasvaitad yadīcchasiVdha
nāpy alpam aparādhaṃ teVdha
karomi tridaśeśvaraVdha
tathāpi vadhayogyaṃ māṃVdha
manyase cet kṣipāyudhamVdha
śrūyate kila govindeVdha
bhaktim udvahatāṃ nṛṇāmVdha
tridaśāḥ paripanthinaḥVdha
tāpaso 'haṃ kva niḥsaṅgaḥVdha
kva ca kopas tavedṛśaḥVdha
vijñātam etad govindaVdha
bhavanti bahavo vighnāVdha
nare śreyaḥparāyaṇeVdha
śreyaś cānyan na vidyateVdha
sa tvaṃ prahara vā mā vāVdha
mayi vajraṃ puraṃdaraVdha
nāham utsṛjya govindamVdha
anyam ārādhayāmi bhoḥVdha
na cāpi vajraṃ vajrī vāVdha
tvaṃ ca nānye surāsurāḥVdha
śaktā nihantum īśāneVdha
hṛdayasthe janārdaneVdha
kiṃ ca no bahunoktenaVdha
nāhaṃ vakṣyāmy ataḥ paraṃVdha
yathepsitaṃ kuruṣva tvaṃVdha
kariṣye 'ham abhīpsitamVdha
evam uktvā surapatiṃVdha
pārthivaḥ sa punas tapaḥVdha
cacāra maunam āsthāyaVdha
tenātuṣyata keśavaḥVdha
saṃdarśayām āsa tataḥVdha
svaṃ vapuḥ kaiṭabhārdanaḥVdha
caturbhujam udārāṅgaṃVdha
kirīṭasragdharaṃ spaṣṭaṃVdha
airāvataś ca garuḍasVdha
tatkṣaṇāt samadṛśyataVdha

pītavāsasam acyutamVdha
vilokya bhaktiśirasāVdha
sahasaiva mahīṃ yayauVdha
pratyuvāca ca bhūpālaḥVdha
praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥVdha
romāñcitatanuḥ stotramVdha
padmanābhaṃ tato 'stuvatVdha
ādideva jayājeyaVdha
jaya sargādikārakaVdha
bṛhanmūrte jayākṣaraVdha
jaya sarvagatācintyaVdha
jaya janmajarāpahaVdha
jaya vyāpiñ jayābhedaVdha
sarvabhūteṣv avasthitaVdha
jaya yajñapate nāthaVdha
jaya vijñātasiddhāntaVdha
māyāmohaka keśavaVdha
lokasthityartham anaghaVdha
varāha jaya bhūdharaVdha
nṛsiṃha jaya devāriVdha
devānām aribhītānāmVdha
ārtināśana vāmanaVdha
jaya krāntasamastorvīVdha
jitaṃ te jagatām īśaVdha
jitaṃ te sarva sarvadaVdha
jitaṃ te sarvabhūteśaVdha
yogidhyeya namo 'stu teVdha
namo 'stv avyapadeśyāyaVdha
namaḥ sūkṣmasvarūpiṇeVdha
namas trimūrtaye tubhyaṃVdha
viśvamūrte namo 'stu teVdha
brahmādyaiś cintyate rūpaṃVdha
yat tat sadasataḥ paraṃVdha
viśeṣair aviśeṣyāyaVdha

puruṣākhyaṃ tato rūpaṃVdha
nirguṇaṃ guṇabhoktṛ caVdha
prakṛteḥ parataḥ sūkṣmaṃVdha
tan namasyāmi te hareVdha
atisūkṣmatamaṃ mahatVdha
prākṛtaṃ tava tad rūpaṃVdha
tasmai deva namāmy ahamVdha
rūpair nānāvidhair yaś caVdha
līlayā vyavahāras teVdha
tasmai devātmane namaḥVdha
prasīda viṣṇo govindaVdha
vāsudeva maheśvaraVdha
itthaṃ stuto jagannāthaḥVdha
proktavān iti keśavaḥVdha
ambarīṣaṃ pṛthivīśaṃVdha
jagat saṃnādayan girāVdha
ambarīṣa prasanno 'smiVdha
bhaktyā stotreṇa cānaghaVdha
varaṃ vṛṇīṣva dharmajñaVdha
yat te manasi vartateVdha
eṣa eva varaḥ ślāghyoVdha
yad dṛṣṭo 'si jagatpateVdha
tvaddarśanam apuṇyānāṃVdha
svapneṣv api hi durlabhamVdha
bālyāt prabhṛti yā devaVdha
tvayi bhaktir mamācyutaVdha
vetti tāṃ bhagavān evaVdha
hṛdisthaḥ sarvadehināmVdha
tvatprasādān mameśānaVdha

kośadaṇḍau tathātīvaVdha
śarīrārogyam uttamamVdha
striyo 'nnapānasāmarthyāVdha
hāniḥ svalpāpi nāsti meVdha
balaṃ nāgasahasrasyaVdha
dhārayāmy arisūdanaVdha
saṃtatir nibhṛtā bhṛtyāVdha
sānurāgāś ca me janāḥVdha
dharmahāniś ca deveśaVdha
na hi me pālane bhuvaḥVdha
yad yad icchāmy ahaṃ tat tatVdha
sarvam asti jagatpateVdha
prasanno bhagavān itiVdha
jñātaṃ mayā hi govindeVdha
nāprasanne vibhūtayaḥVdha
evaṃ sarvasukhāhlādaVdha
madhyastho 'pi ca keśavaVdha
trāsād udvignamānasaḥVdha
mayi prasādābhimukhaṃVdha

niṣkalmaṣo bhavet sadyoVdha

daśāśvamedhāvabhṛthena tulyaḥVdha

tathaiva caitravaiśākhaVdha

prāpte prāpte tu taddineVdha

āṣāḍhe śrāvaṇe māsiVdha
prāpte bhādrapade tathāVdha

kārttikādiṣu māseṣuVdha
tathaivābhyarcya keśavamVdha
bhūtyā samanvitaṃ dadyācVdha
śaśāṅkāyārhanaṃ niśiVdha

tṛtīyam iti pāraṇamVdha
pratipūjāsu dadyāc caVdha

prāśanaṃ kāyaśodhanamVdha
caturaḥ prathamān māsānVdha

kuśodakaṃ tathaivānyadVdha

dāmbhikāḥ śaṭhabuddhayaḥVdha
niḥśaucā vakramatayoVdha
evaṃvidhās te sanmārgādVdha
vedaproktād bahiḥsthitāḥVdha
kriyākalāpaṃ nindantaVdha
ātmānaṃ ca parāṃś caivaVdha
kurvanti narakasthitānVdha
teṣāṃ darśanasaṃbhāṣaVdha
sparśanāni naraiḥ sadāVdha
parityājyāni dṛṣṭe caVdha
proktaḥ saṃbhāṣaṇe ca yaḥVdha
saṃsparśe ca budhaḥ snātvāVdha
śuciḥ śuciṣadaṃ smaretVdha
bhavaty ataḥ sadaivaiṣāmVdha
puṇyakāmo mahābhāgaḥVdha

abhyāso ratir eva caVdha

āsuraṃ bhāvam āśritāḥVdha

aiśvaryāder dvijottamaVdha
yathā manorathair labdhairVdha
vicyutir dharmahānijāVdha

saṃtater devalokataḥVdha
abhīṣṭād anyato vāpiVdha
padād yena na vicyutimVdha
prāpnoti puruṣo brahmanVdha
nārī vāpuṇyasaṃkṣayātVdha
tan mamācakṣva viprarṣeVdha
duḥkham ebhyo hi vicyutiḥVdha
satyam etan mahābhāgaVdha
duḥkhaṃ prāptasya saṃkṣayaḥVdha
aiśvaryād atha vittasyaVdha
bandhuvargasukhasya vāVdha

abhīṣṭair aparais tathāVdha

annaṃ māsacatuṣṭayamVdha
nivedayet kārttikādiVdha
saṃyāvaṃ ca tataḥ paramVdha
āṣāḍhādau ca devāyaVdha
pāyasaṃ vai nivedayetVdha
tenaivānnena viprarṣeVdha

tasyaiva prāśanāc chuciḥVdha

evaṃ saṃvatsarasyānteVdha
tataḥ suptotthite 'cyuteVdha
saṃyak saṃpūjya viprarṣeVdha
tam eva puruṣottamamVdha
praṇamya prārthayed vidvāñVdha
śuciḥ snāto yathāvidhiVdha

pāpasya vṛddhiṃ samupaitu puṇyamVdha
aiśvaryavittādi sadākṣayaṃ meVdha
'kṣayā ca me saṃtatir acyutāstuVdha
yathācyutas tvaṃ parataḥ parasmātVdha
sa brahmabhūtāt parataḥ parātmanVdha
tathācyutaṃ me kuru vāñchitaṃ yanVdha
mayā padaṃ pāpaharāprameyaVdha
acyutānanta govindaVdha
prasīda yad abhīpsitamVdha

nārī tapodhanā bhūtvāVdha

nāhaṃ cirantanān vedmiVdha
devarāja sureśvarānVdha
ātmanaḥ samakālīnaṃVdha
mām avaihi sureśvaraVdha
tataḥ papraccha devendraḥVdha
ko 'smābhir munipuṅgavaVdha

jānāty akhiladevendraVdha
caritaṃ śāmbharāyaṇīVdha

yayau yatra mahābhāgāVdha
tāpasī śāmbharāyaṇīVdha

samyag arghyena saṃpūjyaVdha
praṇipatya śubhavratāVdha
namo 'stu devarājāyaVdha
tathaivāṅgirase namaḥVdha

āvām abhyāgatau praṣṭuṃVdha

yac ca kāryaṃ mahābhāgeVdha
tat pṛṣṭā kathayeha nauVdha
yadi smarasi kalyāṇiVdha
pūrvendracaritāni nauVdha
tadākhyāhi mahābhāgeVdha
devendrasya kutūhalātVdha
yadi śakyaṃ mayā kartuṃVdha
tat kariṣye vimṛṣyatuVdha
yo vai pūrvaḥ surendrasyaVdha
tataś ca prathamo hi yaḥVdha
tasmāt pūrvataro yaś caVdha
tasyāpi prathamāś ca yeVdha
teṣāṃ pūrvatarā ye caVdha
vedmi tān akhilān ahamVdha
teṣāṃ ca caritaṃ kṛtsnaṃVdha
jānāmy āṅgirasāṃ varaVdha
manvantarāṇy anekāniVdha
sṛṣṭiṃ ca tridivaukasāmVdha
saptarṣīn subahūn devaVdha
manūnāṃ ca sutān nṛpaVdha
tat pṛccha tvaṃ vadāmy eṣāVdha
pūrvendracaritaṃ muneVdha
evam ukte tatas tābhyāṃVdha
pṛṣṭā sā śāmbharāyaṇīVdha
yathāvad ācaṣṭa tayoḥVdha
pūrvendracaritaṃ dvijaVdha
svāyambhuve yas tu manauVdha
manau svārociṣe tu yaḥVdha
uttame tāmase caivaVdha
raivate cākṣuṣe tathāVdha
yo yo babhūva devendrasVdha

tayor jagāda caritaṃVdha
yathāvac chāmbharāyaṇīVdha
tataḥ kautūhalaparoVdha

uvāca jānāsi kathaṃVdha

sarva eva hi devendrāḥVdha

dadātv anantaṃ ca punasVdha
tad evāstv anyajanmaniVdha
karoty etan mahāvratamVdha
kurvan mā kṣayam etu caVdha
ity uccāryābhipūjyainaṃVdha
yathāvad vidhinā naraḥVdha
samāhitamanā bhūtvāVdha
viprāya dakṣiṇāṃ dadyādVdha
anantaḥ prīyatām itiVdha
samuccārya tato naktaṃVdha
bhuñjīyāt tailavarjitamVdha
tataś ca pauṣe puṣyarkṣeVdha
tathaiva bhagavatkaṭimVdha
vāmām abhyarcayet kṛtvāVdha
gomūtraprāśanaṃ budhaḥVdha
anantaḥ sarvakāmānāmVdha
iti coccārayed budhaḥVdha
bhuñjīta ca tathā vipraṃVdha
vācayitvā yathāvidhiVdha

bhagavan sarvabhūtātmanVdha

prakṛtiṃ praviśantu meVdha
niṣkevalaṃ padaṃ caivaVdha
prayāmi paramaṃ tavaVdha
ekībhāvas tvayaivāstuVdha
mā me janma bhavet punaḥVdha
namo bhagavate tasmaiVdha
viṣṇave prabhaviṣṇaveVdha
tvanmanas tvadgatapṛāṇasVdha
tvadbhaktas tvatparāyaṇaḥVdha
tvām evānusmare devaVdha
maraṇe pratyupasthiteVdha
pūrvadehakṛtā ye meVdha
vyādhayas te viśantu māmVdha
ārdayantu ca duḥkhāniVdha
pravimuñcāmi yad ṛṇamVdha
upatiṣṭhantu me rogāVdha
ye mayā pūrvasaṃcitāḥVdha
anṛṇo gantum icchāmiVdha
tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padamVdha
ahaṃ bhagavatas tasyaVdha
mama cāsau sureśvaraḥVdha
tasyāhaṃ na praṇaśyāmiVdha
sa ca me na praṇaśyatiVdha
namo bhagavate tasmaiVdha
yena sarvam idaṃ tatamVdha
tam eva ca prapanno 'smiVdha
mama yo yasya cāpy ahamVdha
imām anusmṛtiṃ nityaṃVdha
vaiṣṇavīṃ pāpanāśanīmVdha
svapañ jāgrat paṭhed yas tuVdha
trisaṃdhyaṃ vāpi yaḥ smaretVdha
maraṇe cāpy anuprāpteVdha
yas tv imāṃ samanusmaretVdha
api pāpasamācāraḥVdha
so 'pi yāti parāṃ gatimVdha
arcayann api yo devaṃVdha
gṛhe vāpi baliṃ dadetVdha
juhvad agniṃ smared vāpiVdha

madbhaktaḥ śraddhayānvitaḥVdha

nāsau tat padam āpnotiVdha

tasmāt pradeyaṃ sādhubhyoVdha

yo dadyād bhagavajjñānaṃVdha

na tu tulyaṃ kathaṃcanaVdha
kṛcchreṣv āpatsu saṃbhrameVdha

varāho rakṣatu jaleVdha
viṣameṣu ca vāmanaḥVdha
rāmo rāmaś ca rāmaś caVdha
trāyantāṃ dasyudoṣataḥVdha
aṭavyāṃ nārasiṃhas tuVdha
sarvataḥ pātu keśavaḥVdha
baddhaḥ parikaras tenaVdha

sakṛd uccāritaṃ yenaVdha
harir ity akṣaradvayamVdha

candrasūryādayo grahāḥVdha
adyāpi na nivartanteVdha
na vāsudevāt param asti maṅgalaṃVdha
na vāsudevāt paramaṃ pavitramVdha
na vāsudevāt param asti daivataṃVdha
na vāsudevaṃ praṇipatya sīdatiVdha
tasmān mām eva devarṣeVdha
dhyāyasvātandritaḥ sadāVdha

nāradaḥ pratibodhitaḥVdha
cakāra keśave bhaktiṃVdha
tasmāt tvaṃ kuru bhūpateVdha

yaj japan sugatiṃ yātiVdha

kaścid āsīd dvijadrogdhāVdha

babhūvābhirataṃ manaḥVdha

rākṣasatve viśeṣataḥVdha

tasya pāparatasyaivaṃVdha

tena vai karmadoṣeṇaVdha
nānyā vṛttir arocataVdha

tat tad ādāya rākṣasaḥVdha
cakhāda puruṣavyāghraVdha
bāhugocaram āgatamVdha
evaṃ tasyātiduṣṭasyaVdha
kurvataḥ prāṇināṃ vadhamVdha
jagāma sumahān kālaḥVdha
pariṇāmaṃ tathā vayaḥVdha
sa dadarśa tapasyantaṃVdha
tāpasaṃ saṃśritavratamVdha
ūrdhvabāhuṃ mahābhāgaṃVdha
kṛtarakṣaṃ samantataḥVdha
taṃ dṛṣṭvā sa tu durbuddhirVdha
brāhmaṇaṃ rākṣasādhamaḥVdha
samabhyadhāvad vegenaVdha
samādātuṃ cikhādiṣuḥVdha
tena rakṣā ca yā dikṣuVdha
brāhmaṇenābhavat kṛtāVdha
tayā nirastaṃ tad rakṣoVdha
bhagavan kīdṛśīṃ rakṣāṃVdha
sa cakāra dvijottamaḥVdha
yayā nirdhūtavīryo 'sauVdha
nirasto rajanīcaraḥVdha
ekāgracitto govindeVdha
taj japaṃs tatparāyaṇaḥVdha
tapaś cacāra vipro 'sauVdha

śrotuṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ varaVdha
sadā sarvabhayebhyas tuVdha

tripuraṃ jaghnuṣaḥ pūrvaṃVdha
brahmaṇā viṣṇupañjaraḥVdha
śaṃkarasya kuruśreṣṭhaVdha
rakṣaṇāya nirūpitaḥVdha
vāgīśena tu śakrasyaVdha
balaṃ hantuṃ prayāsyataḥVdha
tasya rūpaṃ pravakṣyāmiVdha
tan nibodha mahīpateVdha
viṣṇuḥ prācyāṃ sthitaś cakrīVdha
viṣṇur dakṣiṇato gadīVdha
pratīcyāṃ śārṅgadhṛg viṣṇurVdha

hṛṣīkeśo vikoṇeṣuVdha

pretā vināyakāḥ krūrāVdha

dandasūkāś ca pannagāḥVdha
sarve bhavantu te saumyāḥVdha
cittavṛttiharā ye meVdha

chāyāvibhraṃśakāś ca yeVdha

mamāstu devadevasyaVdha
vāsudevasya kīrtanātVdha
pṛṣṭhe purastān mama dakṣiṇottareVdha

nyastavān viṣṇupañjaramVdha

rākṣasaḥ punar abravītVdha

sādhv etan manasi sthitamVdha

vedmi nāsyāḥ parāyaṇamVdha

nirvedaṃ prāpitaṃ paramVdha

mayy anukrośam āvahaVdha
yathā pāpāpanodo meVdha
bhavaty ārya tathā kuruVdha

sadayas tena rakṣasāVdha
pratyuvāca mahābhāgaVdha

ṣaṣṭhe kāle na me brahmanVdha
kaścid grahaṇam āgataḥVdha

guror yan na virodhāyaVdha
yan na dharmoparodhakamVdha

namaś ca te kaiṭabhasūdanāyaVdha
svanābhipadmodaraśāyine caVdha
brahmasvarūpopanatāya caivaVdha
sraṣṭre namaḥ pālayitre sthitau caVdha
sarveśa tubhyaṃ puruṣottamāyaVdha
rudrāya cānte kṣayahetave teVdha
nato 'smi saṃhārakarāya viṣṇoVdha
jaya prapannārtiharāprameyaVdha
jayāgnivasvaśvimaya prajeśaVdha
rudrendracandrastuta devadevaVdha
jayāmarāṇām ariśātanāyaVdha
jitaṃ tvayā sarvaga sarvasāraṃVdha
sarvātmabhūtākhila vedavedyaVdha
jitaṃ jitākṣāmalacittadṛśyaVdha
carācarādhāra dharādhareḍyaVdha
yajñāśrayo yajñapumān aśeṣaVdha
deveśa martyāsurayajñabhoktaḥVdha
tvam īḍyamāno 'bhimataṃ dadāsiVdha
dharādhareśācyuta vāsudevaVdha
namas te devadeva tvaṃVdha
yathā pāsy akhilaṃ jagatVdha
sthitau tathā samastebhyoVdha
doṣebhyo māṃ samuddharaVdha
kṛṣṇācyuta hṛṣīkeśaVdha
sarvabhūteśa keśavaVdha
mahātmaṃs trāhi māṃ bhaktaṃVdha
vāsudeva prasīda meVdha

cedirājaṃ tato 'surāḥVdha
jahasuḥ satalākṣepaṃVdha
procuś ca dvijarūpiṇaḥVdha
prājñaḥ kila prajāpālaśVdha

tas asya jñānam akhilaṃVdha
viparītārtham īdṛśamVdha

yo 'nyatras trāṇakāmo vāVdha
yajñabhāgam abhīpsateVdha
sa trātā tava govindoVdha
bhaviṣyaty ativismayaḥVdha
yadā tvaṃ bhagavadbhaktoVdha
vipraśāpān nipātitaḥVdha
tadā sa vāsudevas teVdha
kva gato 'lpaśruto 'vyayaḥVdha
na vāsudevo na harirVdha
na govindo na keśavaḥVdha
śāpaṃ dadatsu vipreṣuVdha
paritrāṇaparo bhavetVdha
sa tvam ārtapralāpebhyoVdha
viramādya yadīcchasiVdha
kubuddhim etāṃ saṃtyajyaVdha
svapauruṣaparo bhavaVdha
na vayaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃVdha
nānantaṃ nācyutaṃ harimVdha
saṃśritā na ca sīdāmaḥVdha
svapauruṣam upāśritāḥVdha
yady asmadvacanaṃ vīraVdha
na mohena viśaṅkaseVdha
tadāśrayasva svaṃ vīryaṃVdha

sa teṣāṃ cedipuṅgavaḥVdha
hṛdayena śuśoca tānVdha
uvāca cedirājo vai hṛdaye kṛtamatsaraḥVdha
aho moho 'yam eteṣāmVdha
yena sarveśvare viṣṇāvVdha

yūyaṃ vayaṃ tathaivānyeVdha

vipākaḥ karmaṇāṃ ca yaḥVdha
saṃśuddhihetuḥ svacchandātVdha

parīkṣāṃ ca jagannāthaḥVdha
karoty adṛḍhacetasāmVdha

yadā janārdane bhaktiṃVdha

garhyate yena keśavaḥVdha

na viṣṇubhakto mantavyaḥVdha

teṣāṃ mayā yad ajñānājVdha

tenāpi tuṣṭa evāhaṃVdha
viṣṇor aṃśā dvijottamāḥVdha
kriyāvān mama poto 'yaṃVdha
bhūtalād yo rasātaleVdha

saṃsāragartād uttāraṃVdha

yathāhaṃ nābhivāñchāmiVdha
bhogān ārādhya keśavamVdha
tena satyena viṣṇur meVdha
sarvadoṣān vyapohatuVdha
yathā na mātā na pitāVdha
nātmā na suhṛdaḥ sutāḥVdha

tathā māṃ pātu keśavaḥVdha
yathā viṣṇumayaṃ sarvamVdha
etat paśyāmy ahaṃ jagatVdha
tathā mama manodoṣānVdha
aśeṣān sa vyapohatuVdha
jātā viṣṇuvilomeṣuVdha
bhavatsv api dayā mamaVdha
yathā tenādya satyenaVdha
bhavantaḥ santu tanmayāḥVdha
yathā nāhaṃ bhavaddveṣānVdha
na saṃharṣād bravīmy ahamVdha
kṛpayaiva tathā sarveVdha
bhavantaḥ santu tanmayāḥVdha
yo yo na bhakto govindeVdha
tatra tatra kṛpā yathāVdha
mamārivarge 'pi tathāVdha
bhaktir vo 'stu janārdaneVdha

devadeve 'py abhūd bhaktirVdha

hṛdaye saṃniveśayaVdha
saṃpūjya yaṃ pūjyatamoVdha
bhavaty atra jagattrayeVdha
tam īśvareśvaraṃ viṣṇuṃVdha
hṛdaye kuru pārthivaVdha
kuru citte janārdanamVdha
eṣa śāstrārthasadbhāvaḥVdha
kim uktair bahuvistaraiḥVdha
yasmin prasannacittas tvaṃVdha
yasmin kopam upaiṣi caVdha
tāv ubhāv api tadbhūtauVdha
cintayan siddhim eṣyasiVdha

prītyā snehena vā tavaVdha

manasaḥ sthairyakāraṇātVdha
svapan vibuddhyann uttiṣṭhanVdha
sthito bhuñjan piban vrajanVdha
sarvagaṃ sarvakartāraṃVdha

yaṃ namasyanti devatāḥVdha

taṃ namasyaṃ namāmy ahamVdha

tathāprītir varānaneVdha
ātmajñānaparāś ca yeVdha

vāṅmanaḥkāyikīṃ hiṃsāṃVdha

paradārāṃś ca ye narāḥVdha

dṛḍhaṃ priyatamāḥ sadāVdha

parāpavādaṃ nindāṃ caVdha
ye na kurvanti puruṣāsVdha

sadaivāhaṃ na durlabhaḥVdha

svadharmād acalan deviVdha

namaskāre pradakṣiṇeVdha

narair ārādhyate hariḥVdha

namaḥ paṅkajanetrāyaVdha
namaḥ paṅkajanābhayeVdha
namaḥ paṅkajasaṃbhūtiVdha

layaṃ ca yasmin pralaye prayāntiVdha
taṃ vāsudevaṃ praṇamāmy acintyamVdha
na yasya rūpaṃ na balaṃ prabhāvoVdha
na ca svabhāvaḥ paramasya puṃsaḥVdha
vijñāyate sarvapitāmahādyaisVdha
taṃ vāsudevaṃ praṇamāmy acintyamVdha
rūpasya cakṣur grahaṇe tvag eṣāVdha
sparśagrahītrī rasanā rasasyaVdha
śrotraṃ ca śabdagrahaṇe narāṇāṃVdha

praṇipatya mahābāhurVdha
yadi sānugrahā buddhirVdha

tad ahaṃ praṣṭum icchāmiVdha
kiṃcit tad vaktum arhathaVdha
bhavadbhir yady ahaṃ na syāṃVdha

jñānāny anyāny asārāṇiVdha
śilpinīva nareśvaraVdha
ekam eva paraṃ jñānaṃVdha
yad yogaprāptikārakamVdha
ahaṃ vaktā bhavāñ śrotāVdha
vācyo yogo vimuktidaḥVdha
prāṇinām upakārāyaVdha

yaś caitān niyatān dharmānVdha
paṭhec chraddhāsamanvitaḥVdha
viṣṇau manaḥ samāveśyaVdha
sarvatra samadarśanaḥVdha
tasya pāpaṃ tathā rogānVdha
yac cānyad duritaṃ kiṃcitVdha
tat sarvaṃ hanti keśavaḥVdha
hemante ya imān dharmāñVdha
śṛṇoti vasudhādhipaVdha
śraddhāsamanvitaḥ samyakVdha
so 'gniṣṭomaphalaṃ labhetVdha
śiśire ca naravyāghraVdha
yaḥ śṛṇoti yathāvidhiVdha
puṇḍarīkasya yajñasyaVdha
sa prāpnoti phalaṃ naraḥVdha
madhumādhavasaṃjñe tuVdha
yaḥ śṛṇoti naras tv imānVdha
so 'śvamedhakrator bhūpaVdha
prāpnoty avikalaṃ phalamVdha
śṛṇvann etān nidāghe caVdha
dharmān dharmabhṛtāṃ varaVdha
vājapeyasya yajñasyaVdha
phalaṃ prāpnoty asaṃśayamVdha
varṣāsu cemān yo dharmānVdha
saṃśṛṇvan vasudhādhipaVdha
rājasūyakratoḥ puṇyamVdha
akhilaṃ samavāpnuyātVdha
śaratkāle ca saṃśṛṇvanVdha
dharmān etān nararṣabhaVdha
prāpnoti gosavaphalaṃVdha
samyak śraddhāsamanvitaḥVdha
ṛtuṣv eteṣv etad evaVdha
paṭhatām api pārthivaVdha
phalaṃ bhavati duṣṭeṣuVdha
graheṣv ete śubhapradāḥVdha
kapilānāṃ śatasyoktaṃVdha
yat phalaṃ jyeṣṭhapuṣkareVdha
bhūyo bhūyas tad āpnotiVdha
pāraṇe pāraṇe gateVdha
bhaktyā paṭhati yaś caitānVdha
devasya purato hareḥVdha
so 'rcayaty avanīpālaVdha
jñānayajñena keśavamVdha
sarvābādhās tathā pāpamVdha
akhilaṃ manujeśvaraVdha
viṣṇudharmā vyapohantiVdha
saṃsmṛtāḥ paṭhitāḥ śrutāḥVdha
etat te sarvam ākhyātaṃVdha
rahasyaṃ paramaṃ hareḥVdha
nātaḥ parataraṃ kiṃcicVdha
śrāvyaṃ śrutisukhāvahamVdha
puruṣasya vipaścitaḥVdha
na durlabhaṃ naravyāghraVdha
paramaṃ brahma śāśvatamVdha
